Rewarding time to end or eliminate a certain number of enemies will trigger new Bouns Times and new enemies.; #r5, the enemies' status will be upgraded with the player level, while the rewards obtained will also be upgraded with the upgrade of the enemies' ability; #r6, if the stage is interrupted for other reasons (including but not limited to the player is dead, the time is ended, the network is offline, the equipment is powered off, etc.), the instance dungeon will be directly ended.
